4. A constant

This means we need a candidate that can produce a **T·ε³** term. Let me check each candidate for this capability.

Most candidates don't involve T at all, or involve T only through terms like `T*c0` (linear in T), `1/T^5`, `exp(c/T)`, `log(T*c + ...)`, or `T^c0`. None of these can produce a T·ε³ cross-term.
